Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")\nelse:\n    print(f"API key available: {api_key[:10]}...")\n    \n    # Multiple search queries to find USGS NAS database and occurrence records\',\n        \'"USGS NAS database" crocodile alligator Florida invasive species\',\n        \'USGS nonindigenous aquatic species crocodile Crocodylus Florida location data\',\n        \'site:nas.er.usgs.gov crocodile species Florida occurrence database\'\n    ]\n    \n    all_search_results = []\n    \n    for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):\n        print(f"\\n=== SEARCH {i}: {query} ===\\n")\n        \n        # Prepare API request parameters\n        params = {\n            "q": query,\n            "api_key": api_key,\n            "engine": "google",\n            "google_domain": "google.com",\n            "safe": "off",\n            "num": 10,\n            "type": "search",\n        }\n        \n        try:\n            # Make API request to SerpAPI\n            response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)\n            \n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                results = response.json()\n                \n                if results.get("organic_results"):\n                    print(f"Found {len(results[\'organic_results\'])} results for query {i}")\n                    \n                    # Analyze results for USGS NAS database and crocodile relevance\n                    usgs_nas_results = []\n                    crocodile_results = []\n                    florida_results = []\n                    \n                    for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"]):\n                        title = result.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                        link = result.get(\'link\', \'No link\')\n                        snippet = result.get(\'snippet\', \'No snippet\')\n                        \n                        print(f"\\nResult {j+1}:")\n                        print(f"Title: {title}")\n                        print(f"Link: {link}")\n                        print(f"Snippet: {snippet[:200]}..." if len(snippet) > 200 else f"Snippet: {snippet}")\n                        \n                        # Check for USGS NAS database relevance\n                        if (\'usgs\' in link.lower() and \'nas\' in link.lower()) or \'nas.er.usgs.gov\' in link.lower():\n                            usgs_nas_results.append(result)\n                            print("*** USGS NAS DATABASE IDENTIFIED ***")\n                        elif \'usgs\' in link.lower() or \'usgs\' in title.lower():\n                            usgs_nas_results.append(result)\n                            print("*** USGS SOURCE IDENTIFIED ***")\n                        \n                        # Check for crocodile species relevance\n                        crocodile_indicators = [\'crocodile\', \'crocodylus\', \'caiman\', \'alligator\', \'reptile\']\n                        if any(indicator in (title + snippet).lower() for indicator in crocodile_indicators):\n                            crocodile_results.append(result)\n                            print("*** CROCODILE/REPTILE CONTENT IDENTIFIED ***")\n                        \n                        # Check for Florida relevance\n                        if \'florida\' in (title + snippet).lower() or \'fl\' in (title + snippet).lower():\n                            florida_results.append(result)\n                            print("*** FLORIDA LOCATION IDENTIFIED ***")\n                        \n                        # Check for database/occurrence relevance\n                        database_indicators = [\'database\', \'occurrence\', \'record\', \'species\', \'nonindigenous\', \'invasive\']\n                        if any(indicator in (title + snippet).lower() for indicator in database_indicators):\n                            print("*** DATABASE/OCCURRENCE CONTENT IDENTIFIED ***")\n                        \n                        print("-" * 60)\n                    \n                    # Store results for this query\n                    query_results = {\n                        \'query\': query,\n                        \'total_results\': len(results[\'organic_results\']),\n                        \'usgs_nas_results\': len(usgs_nas_results),\n                        \'crocodile_results\': len(crocodile_results),\n                        \'florida_results\': len(florida_results),\n                        \'results\': results[\'organic_results\'],\n                        \'top_usgs_nas_links\': [r[\'link\'] for r in usgs_nas_results[:3]],\n                        \'top_crocodile_links\': [r[\'link\'] for r in crocodile_results[:3]],\n                        \'top_florida_links\': [r[\'link\'] for r in florida_results[:3]]\n                    }\n                    \n                    all_search_results.append(query_results)\n                    \n                else:\n                    print(f"No organic results found for query {i}")\n                    if \'error\' in results:\n                        print(f"API Error: {results[\'error\']}")\n                        \n            else:\n                print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error during search {i}: {e}")\n    \n    # Save comprehensive search results\n    search_data = {\n        \'target_objective\': {\n counts\',\n                \'Verification status\',\n                \'Total number of nonindigenous crocodiles documented\'\n            ]\n        },\n        \'search_queries_used\': search_queries,\n        \'total_searches_conducted\': len(search_queries),\n        \'search_results_by_query\': all_search_results,\n        \'summary\': {\n            \'total_results_found\': sum(len(qr.get(\'results\', [])) for qr in all_search_results),\n            \'usgs_nas_sources_identified\': sum(qr.get(\'usgs_nas_results\', 0) for qr in all_search_results),\n            \'crocodile_content_sources\': sum(qr.get(\'crocodile_results\', 0) for qr in all_search_results),\n            \'florida_location_sources\': sum(qr.get(\'florida_results\', 0) for qr in all_search_results)\n        }\n    }\n    \n    with open(\'workspace/usgs_nas_crocodile_search_results.json\', \'w\') as f:\n        json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2)\n    \n    print(f"\\n===     headers_list = [cell.get_text().strip() for cell in header_cells]\n                                    print(f"  Headers: {headers_list}")\n                                    \n
